<ApiMember kind="function" name="lv_obj_set_style_width" file="core/lv_obj_style_gen.h" line={1815} url="https://github.com/lvgl/lvgl/blob/master/src/core/lv_obj_style_gen.h#L1815">

### lv_obj_set_style_width

Sets width of Widget. Pixel, percentage and <ApiLink name="LV_SIZE_CONTENT" /> values can be used. Percentage values are relative to the width of the parent's content area. Default: Widget dependent, inherited: No, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_width(lv_obj_t *obj, int32_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

<span className="sr-only">Parameters</span>

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| `obj` | <ApiLink name="lv_obj_t" display="lv_obj_t *" /> | Pointer to Widget |
| `value` | <ApiLink name="int32_t" /> | Value to submit |
| `selector` | <ApiLink name="lv_style_selector_t" /> | A joint type for <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" /> and <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" />. Example values:
- `0`: means <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_MAIN" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_DEFAULT" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_KNOB" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_KNOB" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_CHECKED" /> |


</ApiMember>

<ApiMember kind="function" name="lv_obj_set_style_min_width" file="core/lv_obj_style_gen.h" line={1829} url="https://github.com/lvgl/lvgl/blob/master/src/core/lv_obj_style_gen.h#L1829">

### lv_obj_set_style_min_width

Sets a minimal width. Pixel and percentage values can be used. Percentage values are relative to the width of the parent's content area. Default: 0, inherited: No, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_min_width(lv_obj_t *obj, int32_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

### lv_obj_set_style_max_width

Sets a maximal width. Pixel and percentage values can be used. Percentage values are relative to the width of the parent's content area. Default: LV_COORD_MAX, inherited: No, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_max_width(lv_obj_t *obj, int32_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

### lv_obj_set_style_height

Sets height of Widget. Pixel, percentage and <ApiLink name="LV_SIZE_CONTENT" /> can be used. Percentage values are relative to the height of the parent's content area. Default: Widget dependent, inherited: No, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_height(lv_obj_t *obj, int32_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

<ApiMember kind="function" name="lv_obj_set_style_length" file="core/lv_obj_style_gen.h" line={1899} url="https://github.com/lvgl/lvgl/blob/master/src/core/lv_obj_style_gen.h#L1899">

### lv_obj_set_style_length

Its meaning depends on the type of Widget. For example in case of lv_scale it means the length of the ticks. Default: 0, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: Yes.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_length(lv_obj_t *obj, int32_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

<span className="sr-only">Parameters</span>

| Name | Type | Description |

| `selector` | <ApiLink name="lv_style_selector_t" /> | A joint type for <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" /> and <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" />. Example values:
- `0`: means <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_MAIN" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_DEFAULT" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />

<ApiMember kind="function" name="lv_obj_set_style_x" file="core/lv_obj_style_gen.h" line={1914} url="https://github.com/lvgl/lvgl/blob/master/src/core/lv_obj_style_gen.h#L1914">

### lv_obj_set_style_x

Set X coordinate of Widget considering the `align` setting. Pixel and percentage values can be used. Percentage values are relative to the width of the parent's content area. Default: 0, inherited: No, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_x(lv_obj_t *obj, int32_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

<span className="sr-only">Parameters</span>

| `selector` | <ApiLink name="lv_style_selector_t" /> | A joint type for <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" /> and <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" />. Example values:
- `0`: means <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_MAIN" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_DEFAULT" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />

### lv_obj_set_style_y

Set Y coordinate of Widget considering the `align` setting. Pixel and percentage values can be used. Percentage values are relative to the height of the parent's content area. Default: 0, inherited: No, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_y(lv_obj_t *obj, int32_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

<span className="sr-only">Parameters</span>

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| `obj` | <ApiLink name="lv_obj_t" display="lv_obj_t *" /> | Pointer to Widget |
| `value` | <ApiLink name="int32_t" /> | Value to submit |
| `selector` | <ApiLink name="lv_style_selector_t" /> | A joint type for <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" /> and <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" />. Example values:
- `0`: means <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_MAIN" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_DEFAULT" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_KNOB" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_KNOB" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_CHECKED" /> |

<ApiMember kind="function" name="lv_obj_set_style_align" file="core/lv_obj_style_gen.h" line={1947} url="https://github.com/lvgl/lvgl/blob/master/src/core/lv_obj_style_gen.h#L1947">

### lv_obj_set_style_align

Set the alignment which tells from which point of the parent the X and Y coordinates should be interpreted. Possible values are: <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_DEFAULT" />, `LV_ALIGN_TOP_LEFT/MID/RIGHT`, `LV_ALIGN_BOTTOM_LEFT/MID/RIGHT`, `LV_ALIGN_LEFT/RIGHT_MID`, <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_CENTER" />. <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_DEFAULT" /> means <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_TOP_LEFT" /> with LTR base direction and <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_TOP_RIGHT" /> with RTL base direction. Default: <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_DEFAULT" />, inherited: No, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_align(lv_obj_t *obj, lv_align_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

<span className="sr-only">Parameters</span>

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| `obj` | <ApiLink name="lv_obj_t" display="lv_obj_t *" /> | Pointer to Widget |
| `value` | <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" /> | Value to submit |
| `selector` | <ApiLink name="lv_style_selector_t" /> | A joint type for <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" /> and <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" />. Example values:
- `0`: means <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_MAIN" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_DEFAULT" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />

### lv_obj_set_style_bg_opa

Set opacity of the background. Value 0, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_0" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" /> means fully transparent, 255, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_100" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" /> means fully covering, other values or LV_OPA_10, LV_OPA_20, etc means semi transparency. Default: <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" />, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.


### lv_obj_set_style_bg_grad

Set gradient definition. The pointed instance must exist while Widget is alive. NULL to disable. It wraps `BG_GRAD_COLOR`, `BG_GRAD_DIR`, `BG_MAIN_STOP` and `BG_GRAD_STOP` into one descriptor and allows creating gradients with more colors as well. If it's set other gradient related properties will be ignored. Default: `NULL`, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_bg_grad(lv_obj_t *obj, const lv_grad_dsc_t *value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

<span className="sr-only">Parameters</span>

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| `obj` | <ApiLink name="lv_obj_t" display="lv_obj_t *" /> | Pointer to Widget |
| `value` | <ApiLink name="lv_grad_dsc_t" display="const lv_grad_dsc_t *" /> | Pointer to gradient descriptor |
| `selector` | <ApiLink name="lv_style_selector_t" /> | A joint type for <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" /> and <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" />. Example values:
- `0`: means <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_MAIN" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_DEFAULT" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_KNOB" />
- <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_KNOB" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_PRESSED" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_CHECKED" /> |

### lv_obj_set_style_bg_image_opa

Set opacity of the background image. Value 0, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_0" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" /> means fully transparent, 255, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_100" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" /> means fully covering, other values or LV_OPA_10, LV_OPA_20, etc means semi transparency. ### lv_obj_set_style_image_colorkey

Set image colorkey definition. The <ApiLink name="lv_image_colorkey_t" /> contains two color values: `high_color` and `low_color`. the color of pixels ranging from `low_color` to `high_color` will be transparent. Default: `NULL`, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_set_style_text_opa

Set opacity of text. Value 0, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_0" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" /> means fully transparent, 255, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_100" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" /> means fully covering, other values or LV_OPA_10, LV_OPA_20, etc means semi transparency. Default: <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" />, inherited: Yes, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_set_style_text_align

Set how to align the lines of the text. Note that it doesn't align the Widget itself, only the lines inside the Widget. Possible values are `LV_TEXT_ALIGN_LEFT/CENTER/RIGHT/AUTO`. <ApiLink name="lv_text_align_t" display="LV_TEXT_ALIGN_AUTO" /> detect the text base direction and uses left or right alignment accordingly. Default: <ApiLink name="lv_text_align_t" display="LV_TEXT_ALIGN_AUTO" />, inherited: Yes, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
void lv_obj_set_style_text_align(lv_obj_t *obj, lv_text_align_t value, lv_style_selector_t selector)
```

| `selector` | <ApiLink name="lv_style_selector_t" /> | A joint type for <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" /> and <ApiLink name="lv_state_t" />. Example values:
- `0`: means <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" display="LV_PART_MAIN" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_state_t" display="LV_STATE_DEFAULT" />

### lv_obj_set_style_blur_backdrop

If <ApiLink name="true" /> the background of the widget will be blurred. The part should have \< 100% opacity to make it visible. If <ApiLink name="false" /> the given part will be blurred when it's rendered but before drawing the children. Default: <ApiLink name="false" />, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_set_style_blur_quality

Setting to <ApiLink name="lv_blur_quality_t" display="LV_BLUR_QUALITY_SPEED" /> the blurring algorithm will prefer speed over quality. <ApiLink name="lv_blur_quality_t" display="LV_BLUR_QUALITY_PRECISION" /> will force using higher quality but slower blur. With <ApiLink name="lv_blur_quality_t" display="LV_BLUR_QUALITY_AUTO" /> the quality will be selected automatically. Default: <ApiLink name="lv_blur_quality_t" display="LV_BLUR_QUALITY_AUTO" />, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_set_style_opa

Scale down all opacity values of the Widget by this factor. Value 0, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_0" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" /> means fully transparent, 255, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_100" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" /> means fully covering, other values or LV_OPA_10, LV_OPA_20, etc means semi transparency. Default: <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" />, inherited: Yes, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_set_style_recolor_opa

Sets the intensity of color mixing. Value 0, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_0" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" /> means fully transparent. A value of 255, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_100" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" /> means fully opaque. Intermediate values like LV_OPA_10, LV_OPA_20, etc result in semi-transparency. Default: <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" />, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_set_style_rotary_sensitivity

Adjust sensitivity for rotary encoders in 1/256 unit. It means, 128: slow down the rotary to half, 512: speeds up to double, 256: no change. Default: `256`, inherited: Yes, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_get_style_width

### lv_obj_get_style_align

Get the alignment which tells from which point of the parent the X and Y coordinates should be interpreted. Possible values are: <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_DEFAULT" />, `LV_ALIGN_TOP_LEFT/MID/RIGHT`, `LV_ALIGN_BOTTOM_LEFT/MID/RIGHT`, `LV_ALIGN_LEFT/RIGHT_MID`, <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_CENTER" />. <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_DEFAULT" /> means <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_TOP_LEFT" /> with LTR base direction and <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_TOP_RIGHT" /> with RTL base direction. Default: <ApiLink name="lv_align_t" display="LV_ALIGN_DEFAULT" />, inherited: No, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

```c
static lv_align_t lv_obj_get_style_align(const lv_obj_t *obj, lv_part_t part)
```

### lv_obj_get_style_bg_grad

Get gradient definition. The pointed instance must exist while Widget is alive. NULL to disable. It wraps `BG_GRAD_COLOR`, `BG_GRAD_DIR`, `BG_MAIN_STOP` and `BG_GRAD_STOP` into one descriptor and allows creating gradients with more colors as well. If it's set other gradient related properties will be ignored. Default: `NULL`, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

```c
static const lv_grad_dsc_t * lv_obj_get_style_bg_grad(const lv_obj_t *obj, lv_part_t part)
```

<span className="sr-only">Parameters</span>

| Name | Type | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| `obj` | <ApiLink name="lv_obj_t" display="const lv_obj_t *" /> | Pointer to Widget |
| `part` | <ApiLink name="lv_part_t" /> | One of the `LV_PART_...` enum values |


</ApiMember>

### lv_obj_get_style_bg_image_recolor_opa

Get intensity of background image recoloring. Value 0, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_0" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" /> means no mixing, 255, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_100" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" /> means full recoloring, other values or LV_OPA_10, LV_OPA_20, etc are interpreted proportionally. ### lv_obj_get_style_border_side

Get only which side(s) the border should be drawn. Possible values are `LV_BORDER_SIDE_NONE/TOP/BOTTOM/LEFT/RIGHT/INTERNAL`. OR-ed values can be used as well, e.g. <ApiLink name="lv_border_side_t" display="LV_BORDER_SIDE_TOP" />` | `<ApiLink name="lv_border_side_t" display="LV_BORDER_SIDE_LEFT" />. Default: <ApiLink name="lv_border_side_t" display="LV_BORDER_SIDE_FULL" />, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_get_style_text_opa

### lv_obj_get_style_text_align

Get how to align the lines of the text. Note that it doesn't align the Widget itself, only the lines inside the Widget. Possible values are `LV_TEXT_ALIGN_LEFT/CENTER/RIGHT/AUTO`. <ApiLink name="lv_text_align_t" display="LV_TEXT_ALIGN_AUTO" /> detect the text base direction and uses left or right alignment accordingly. Default: <ApiLink name="lv_text_align_t" display="LV_TEXT_ALIGN_AUTO" />, inherited: Yes, layout: Yes, ext. draw: No.

### lv_obj_get_style_blur_backdrop

If <ApiLink name="true" /> the background of the widget will be blurred. The part should have \< 100% opacity to make it visible. If <ApiLink name="false" /> the given part will be blurred when it's rendered but before drawing the children. Default: <ApiLink name="false" />, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.


### lv_obj_get_style_blur_quality

Setting to <ApiLink name="lv_blur_quality_t" display="LV_BLUR_QUALITY_SPEED" /> the blurring algorithm will prefer speed over quality. <ApiLink name="lv_blur_quality_t" display="LV_BLUR_QUALITY_PRECISION" /> will force using higher quality but slower blur. With <ApiLink name="lv_blur_quality_t" display="LV_BLUR_QUALITY_AUTO" /> the quality will be selected automatically. Default: <ApiLink name="lv_blur_quality_t" display="LV_BLUR_QUALITY_AUTO" />, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.


### lv_obj_get_style_opa

Scale down all opacity values of the Widget by this factor. Value 0, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_0" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" /> means fully transparent, 255, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_100" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" /> means fully covering, other values or LV_OPA_10, LV_OPA_20, etc means semi transparency. Default: <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" />, inherited: Yes, layout: No, ext. draw: No.


### lv_obj_get_style_recolor_opa

Gets the intensity of color mixing. Value 0, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_0" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" /> means fully transparent. A value of 255, <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_100" /> or <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_COVER" /> means fully opaque. Intermediate values like LV_OPA_10, LV_OPA_20, etc result in semi-transparency. Default: <ApiLink name="_lv_opacity_level_t" display="LV_OPA_TRANSP" />, inherited: No, layout: No, ext. draw: No.
